- (4): 本文采用的方法包括使用不同机器学习技术来评估ApisTox数据集，分析其独特性并比较其与医学数据集的差异。

- (5): 该研究聚焦于二元分类任务，即区分毒性与非毒性分子，虽然实现了有效的分类能力，但仍指出当前模型的局限性，表明在农药毒性预测领域仍需进一步改进。


## Solving the Best Subset Selection Problem via Suboptimal Algorithms
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24300v1
- **Authors**: ['Vikram Singh', 'Min Sun']
- **Abstrat**: Best subset selection in linear regression is well known to be nonconvex and computationally challenging to solve, as the number of possible subsets grows rapidly with increasing dimensionality of the problem. As a result, finding the global optimal solution via an exact optimization method for a problem with dimensions of 1000s may take an impractical amount of CPU time. This suggests the importance of finding suboptimal procedures that can provide good approximate solutions using much less computational effort than exact methods. In this work, we introduce a new procedure and compare it with other popular suboptimal algorithms to solve the best subset selection problem. Extensive computational experiments using synthetic and real data have been performed. The results provide insights into the performance of these methods in different data settings. The new procedure is observed to be a competitive suboptimal algorithm for solving the best subset selection problem for high-dimensional data.


**Translated Abstract**: 

最佳子集选择（Best subset selection）在线性回归中被广泛认为是非凸的且计算上具有挑战性的，由于问题的维度增加，可能的子集数量迅速增长。因此，对于维度达到数千的问题，通过精确优化方法找到全局最优解可能需要不切实际的计算时间。这表明寻找能够提供良好近似解的次优程序的重要性，这些程序所需的计算工作量远小于精确方法。在这项工作中，我们介绍了一种新程序，并将其与其他流行的次优算法进行了比较。通过使用合成和真实数据进行广泛的计算实验，结果提供了不同数据环境下这些方法性能的洞察。观察到新程序是解决高维数据的最佳子集选择问题的一个具有竞争力的次优算法。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是最佳子集选择在高维线性回归中具有非凸性和计算复杂性，随着维度的增加，可能的子集数量呈指数增长，导致精确方法求解时成本高昂。

- (2): 过去的方法包括前向选择（Forward Selection）、后向选择（Backward Selection）等，但它们在高维情况下处理计算复杂度时面临挑战。本文提出的新方法相较于现有方法通过设计更高效的次优算法，旨在提供更快速的近似解，从而有效解决了这些问题。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出了一种新的次优算法，并通过与其他四种流行的次优算法进行了比较，验证了新算法在高维数据处理中的有效性。

- (4): 本文采用的研究方法是通过广泛的计算实验，包括合成数据和真实数据，对所提议的新算法与现有算法进行比较，从而评估其性能。

- (5): 本文在解决最佳子集选择任务上取得了显著的性能，实验证明了新算法的竞争力，支持了其研究目标的实现。


## Fair Dynamic Spectrum Access via Fully Decentralized Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24296v1
- **Authors**: ['Yubo Zhang', 'Pedro Botelho', 'Trevor Gordon', 'Gil Zussman', 'Igor Kadota']
- **Abstrat**: We consider a decentralized wireless network with several source-destination pairs sharing a limited number of orthogonal frequency bands. Sources learn to adapt their transmissions (specifically, their band selection strategy) over time, in a decentralized manner, without sharing information with each other. Sources can only observe the outcome of their own transmissions (i.e., success or collision), having no prior knowledge of the network size or of the transmission strategy of other sources. The goal of each source is to maximize their own throughput while striving for network-wide fairness. We propose a novel fully decentralized Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based solution that achieves fairness without coordination. The proposed Fair Share RL (FSRL) solution combines: (i) state augmentation with a semi-adaptive time reference; (ii) an architecture that leverages risk control and time difference likelihood; and (iii) a fairness-driven reward structure. We evaluate FSRL in more than 50 network settings with different number of agents, different amounts of available spectrum, in the presence of jammers, and in an ad-hoc setting. Simulation results suggest that, when we compare FSRL with a common baseline RL algorithm from the literature, FSRL can be up to 89.0% fairer (as measured by Jain's fairness index) in stringent settings with several sources and a single frequency band, and 48.1% fairer on average.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们考虑一个去中心化的无线网络，其中多个源-目的对共享有限数量的正交频段。源在去中心化的模式下学习如何随时间适应其传输（具体来说，是其频段选择策略），而无需彼此共享信息。源只能观察到自己传输的结果（即成功或碰撞），对网络大小或其他源的传输策略没有先验知识。每个源的目标是最大化自身的吞吐量，同时努力实现网络整体的公平性。我们提出了一种新颖的完全去中心化的强化学习（RL）解决方案，在没有协调的情况下实现公平。所提出的公平共享RL（FSRL）解决方案结合了：（i）具有半自适应时间参考的状态增强；（ii）利用风险控制和时间差异似然性的架构；以及（iii）以公平性驱动的奖励结构。我们在50多个网络设置中评估FSRL，网络中有不同数量的代理，频谱的可用量不同，存在干扰者，并在自组网设置中进行评估。模拟结果表明，与文献中一种常见的基线RL算法相比，FSRL在源数量较多且频段有限的严格环境中公平性最多提高了89.0%（根据Jain的公平性指数测量），并在平均情况下提高了48.1%公平性。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究了去中心化的无线网络中，多个源-目的对在有限频段内进行动态频谱接入（DSA）的公平性问题。

- (2): 过去的方法主要有集中训练和信息共享，存在需要协调或共享信息的问题。而所提出的方式是完全去中心化的FSRL，代理只观察自身传输结果，能够在无协调情况下实现公平性。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于开发了一种无信息共享的去中心化DSA算法FSRL，能够在随机环境中有效实现公平性。

- (4): 本文提出的方法在状态增强、风险控制和公平性奖励结构方面进行了创新，确保代理在没有其他信息的情况下学习。

- (5): 该方法在多种网络情境下进行评估，表现出在严格环境中可提高高达89%的公平性，支持了其实现公平性的目标。


## Open-Reasoner-Zero: An Open Source Approach to Scaling Up Reinforcement Learning on the Base Model
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24290v1
- **Authors**: ['Jingcheng Hu', 'Yinmin Zhang', 'Qi Han', 'Daxin Jiang', 'Xiangyu Zhang', 'Heung-Yeung Shum']
- **Abstrat**: We introduce Open-Reasoner-Zero, the first open source implementation of large-scale reasoning-oriented RL training focusing on scalability, simplicity and accessibility. Through extensive experiments, we demonstrate that a minimalist approach, vanilla PPO with GAE ($\lambda=1$, $\gamma=1$) and straightforward rule-based rewards, without any KL regularization, is sufficient to scale up both response length and benchmark performance, similar to the phenomenon observed in DeepSeek-R1-Zero. Using the same base model as DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Qwen-32B, our implementation achieves superior performance on AIME2024, MATH500, and the GPQA Diamond benchmark while demonstrating remarkable efficiency -- requiring only a tenth of the training steps, compared to DeepSeek-R1-Zero pipeline. In the spirit of open source, we release our source code, parameter settings, training data, and model weights across various sizes.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们介绍了Open-Reasoner-Zero，这是第一个开源实现的大规模面向推理的强化学习训练，重点关注可扩展性、简单性和可获取性。通过广泛的实验，我们证明了一种极简主义的方法，即使用vanilla PPO与GAE（𝜆 = 1，𝛾 = 1）和简单的基于规则的奖励，不需要任何KL正则化，足以提升响应长度和基准性能，类似于在DeepSeek-R1-Zero中观察到的现象。使用与DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Qwen-32B相同的基础模型，我们的实现在线上任务AIME2024、MATH500和GPQA Diamond基准上实现了卓越的性能，同时展现了显著的效率——所需的训练步骤仅为DeepSeek-R1-Zero管道的十分之一。秉持开源的精神，我们发布了我们的源代码、参数设置、训练数据和不同大小的模型权重。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是大规模强化学习（RL）在语言模型推理任务中的应用，特别是针对复杂问题解决能力的提升。

- (2): 过去的方法（如DeepSeek-R1-Zero）已展示出训练时间的可扩展性，但在实现过程中遇到训练不稳定、响应长度停滞和基准表现平台期等问题。本文提出的方式通过采用vanilla PPO与GAE（𝜆 = 1，𝛾 = 1）以及简单的奖励机制，简化了训练流程，有效应对这些问题，展示了高效性与可扩展性。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提供了一个全面的开源实现，包括大规模强化学习训练的代码、参数设置和数据，推广可重复的研究实践。

- (4): 本文提出的研究方法论是直接从基础模型开始进行大规模的推理导向的强化学习训练，通过精心设计的数据集和奖励机制，提高模型在推理任务上的表现。

- (5): 本文的方法在AIME2024、MATH500和GPQA Diamond基准测试上表现卓越，仅需其训练步骤的十分之一，支持了提升大规模推理能力的目标。


## Evil twins are not that evil: Qualitative insights into machine-generated prompts
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2412.08127v3
- **Authors**: ['Nathanaël Carraz Rakotonirina', 'Corentin Kervadec', 'Francesca Franzon', 'Marco Baroni']
- **Abstrat**: It has been widely observed that language models (LMs) respond in predictable ways to algorithmically generated prompts that are seemingly unintelligible. This is both a sign that we lack a full understanding of how LMs work, and a practical challenge, because opaqueness can be exploited for harmful uses of LMs, such as jailbreaking. We present the first thorough analysis of opaque machine-generated prompts, or autoprompts, pertaining to 6 LMs of different sizes and families. We find that machine-generated prompts are characterized by a last token that is often intelligible and strongly affects the generation. A small but consistent proportion of the previous tokens are prunable, probably appearing in the prompt as a by-product of the fact that the optimization process fixes the number of tokens. The remaining tokens fall into two categories: filler tokens, which can be replaced with semantically unrelated substitutes, and keywords, that tend to have at least a loose semantic relation with the generation, although they do not engage in well-formed syntactic relations with it. Additionally, human experts can reliably identify the most influential tokens in an autoprompt a posteriori, suggesting these prompts are not entirely opaque. Finally, some of the ablations we applied to autoprompts yield similar effects in natural language inputs, suggesting that autoprompts emerge naturally from the way LMs process linguistic inputs in general.





## Value of Information-based Deceptive Path Planning Under Adversarial Interventions
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24284v1
- **Authors**: ['Wesley A. Suttle', 'Jesse Milzman', 'Mustafa O. Karabag', 'Brian M. Sadler', 'Ufuk Topcu']
- **Abstrat**: Existing methods for deceptive path planning (DPP) address the problem of designing paths that conceal their true goal from a passive, external observer. Such methods do not apply to problems where the observer has the ability to perform adversarial interventions to impede the path planning agent. In this paper, we propose a novel Markov decision process (MDP)-based model for the DPP problem under adversarial interventions and develop new value of information (VoI) objectives to guide the design of DPP policies. Using the VoI objectives we propose, path planning agents deceive the adversarial observer into choosing suboptimal interventions by selecting trajectories that are of low informational value to the observer. Leveraging connections to the linear programming theory for MDPs, we derive computationally efficient solution methods for synthesizing policies for performing DPP under adversarial interventions. In our experiments, we illustrate the effectiveness of the proposed solution method in achieving deceptiveness under adversarial interventions and demonstrate the superior performance of our approach to both existing DPP methods and conservative path planning approaches on illustrative gridworld problems.


**Translated Abstract**: 

现有的欺骗路径规划（DPP）方法解决了设计路径以隐瞒其真实目标的問題，适用于一个被动的外部观察者。 然而，这些方法不适用于观察者能够进行对抗性干预以阻碍路径规划代理的问题。 在本文中，我们提出了一种新颖的基于马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）的DPP模型，并开发了新的信息价值（VoI）目标来指导DPP策略的设计。 利用我们提出的VoI目标，路径规划代理通过选择对观察者的信息价值较低的轨迹来欺骗对抗性观察者，使其选择次优干预。 通过利用与线性规划理论的联系，我们推导出了计算上高效的解决方法，以合成在对抗性干预下进行DPP的策略。 在实验中，我们展示了所提解决方法在对抗性干预下实现欺骗性的有效性，并证明了我们的方法比现有的DPP方法和保守的路径规划方法在示例网格世界问题上的更优表现。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景在于开发针对观察者能够进行对抗性干预的欺骗路径规划策略，以解决传统方法在被动观察者情况下的局限性。

- (2): 过去的方法主要集中于被动观察者模型，不考虑观察者可以干预的情境，这让这些方法的适用性受到限制。 本文提出的方法通过引入针对对抗干预的MDP模型和信息价值（VoI）目标，对现有方法进行了扩展。 这种方法解决了缺乏有效 DPP 模型、欺骗度量和解决程序的问题，其动机也很明确。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出了一种新颖的基于MDP的DPP模型，开发了新的VoI度量标准，并提出了高效的线性规划解决方法，从而显著提升了在对抗性设置下的路径规划能力。

- (4): 本文提出的研究方法包括建立MDP模型以结合对抗干预，构建VoI欺骗度量，并通过线性规划求解这些新模型。

- (5): 本文的方法在网格世界问题上进行了实验，表明在真实干预下，新方法的路径成本低于保守的路径规划方法和被动观察者方法。 这一性能结果支持了他们实现更好路径规划目标的愿望。


## PharmAgents: Building a Virtual Pharma with Large Language Model Agents
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.22164v2
- **Authors**: ['Bowen Gao', 'Yanwen Huang', 'Yiqiao Liu', 'Wenxuan Xie', 'Wei-Ying Ma', 'Ya-Qin Zhang', 'Yanyan Lan']
- **Abstrat**: The discovery of novel small molecule drugs remains a critical scientific challenge with far-reaching implications for treating diseases and advancing human health. Traditional drug development--especially for small molecule therapeutics--is a highly complex, resource-intensive, and time-consuming process that requires multidisciplinary collaboration. Recent breakthroughs in artificial intelligence (AI), particularly the rise of large language models (LLMs), present a transformative opportunity to streamline and accelerate this process. In this paper, we introduce PharmAgents, a virtual pharmaceutical ecosystem driven by LLM-based multi-agent collaboration. PharmAgents simulates the full drug discovery workflow--from target discovery to preclinical evaluation--by integrating explainable, LLM-driven agents equipped with specialized machine learning models and computational tools. Through structured knowledge exchange and automated optimization, PharmAgents identifies potential therapeutic targets, discovers promising lead compounds, enhances binding affinity and key molecular properties, and performs in silico analyses of toxicity and synthetic feasibility. Additionally, the system supports interpretability, agent interaction, and self-evolvement, enabling it to refine future drug designs based on prior experience. By showcasing the potential of LLM-powered multi-agent systems in drug discovery, this work establishes a new paradigm for autonomous, explainable, and scalable pharmaceutical research, with future extensions toward comprehensive drug lifecycle management.


**Translated Abstract**: 

新型小分子药物的发现仍然是一个重要的科学挑战，对治疗疾病和改善人类健康具有深远的影响。传统药物开发，特别是针对小分子治疗的药物开发，过程非常复杂、资源密集且耗时长，需要多学科的协作。人工智能（AI）最近的突破，尤其是大型语言模型（LLMs）的兴起，为简化和加速这一过程提供了变革性的机会。本文介绍了PharmAgents，一个由LLM驱动的多智能体协作构建的虚拟制药生态系统。PharmAgents模拟从靶点发现到临床前评估的完整药物发现工作流程，通过集成可解释的LLM驱动代理，配备专业的机器学习模型和计算工具。通过结构化的知识交流和自动优化，PharmAgents识别潜在的治疗靶点，发现有前景的先导化合物，增强结合亲和力和关键分子特性，并进行毒性和合成可行性等的计算分析。此外，该系统支持可解释性、代理交互和自我演变，使其能够根据以往经验优化未来的药物设计。通过展示LLM驱动的多代理系统在药物发现中的潜力，本文建立了一个新的范式，用于自主、可解释和可扩展的制药研究，并将来扩展到全面的药物生命周期管理。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究背景是新型小分子药物发现面临的复杂性、资源密集和耗时等问题，以及现有药物开发方法的高淘汰率和成本上升。

- (2): 过去的方法包括高通量筛选和计算建模，这些方法各自独立地运行，缺乏必要的整合和可解释性。提出的方法PharmAgents通过大型语言模型（LLM）驱动的多智能体协作，解决了传统方法中的整合问题，加强了各阶段的协作与自动化，提升了可解释性。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出了PharmAgents，一个全新的虚拟制药生态系统，它利用LLMs和多智能体系统变革药物发现过程，展示了自主、可解释和高效的药物研究新范式。

- (4): 本文的方法论包括将药物发现流程分解为四个关键阶段，并为每个阶段设计专门的智能代理，这些代理利用LLM和机器学习模型进行协作，从靶点发现到临床前评估的完整模拟。

- (5): 在靶点发现、先导化合物生成及优化、毒性评估等任务上，PharmAgents显著提升了成功率，从原来的15.72%提高到37.94%，并且在合成可行性和毒性评估方面表现出色，表明其性能支持了研究目标。


## Evaluating and Designing Sparse Autoencoders by Approximating Quasi-Orthogonality
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24277v1
- **Authors**: ['Sewoong Lee', 'Adam Davies', 'Marc E. Canby', 'Julia Hockenmaier']
- **Abstrat**: Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have emerged as a workhorse of modern mechanistic interpretability, but leading SAE approaches with top-$k$ style activation functions lack theoretical grounding for selecting the hyperparameter $k$. SAEs are based on the linear representation hypothesis (LRH), which assumes that the representations of large language models (LLMs) are linearly encoded, and the superposition hypothesis (SH), which states that there can be more features in the model than its dimensionality. We show that, based on the formal definitions of the LRH and SH, the magnitude of sparse feature vectors (the latent representations learned by SAEs of the dense embeddings of LLMs) can be approximated using their corresponding dense vector with a closed-form error bound. To visualize this, we propose the ZF plot, which reveals a previously unknown relationship between LLM hidden embeddings and SAE feature vectors, allowing us to make the first empirical measurement of the extent to which feature vectors of pre-trained SAEs are over- or under-activated for a given input. Correspondingly, we introduce Approximate Feature Activation (AFA), which approximates the magnitude of the ground-truth sparse feature vector, and propose a new evaluation metric derived from AFA to assess the alignment between inputs and activations. We also leverage AFA to introduce a novel SAE architecture, the top-AFA SAE, leading to SAEs that: (a) are more in line with theoretical justifications; and (b) obviate the need to tune SAE sparsity hyperparameters. Finally, we empirically demonstrate that top-AFA SAEs achieve reconstruction loss comparable to that of state-of-the-art top-k SAEs, without requiring the hyperparameter $k$ to be tuned. Our code is available at: https://github.com/SewoongLee/top-afa-sae.


**Translated Abstract**: 

稀疏自编码器（SAEs）已成为现代机制可解释性的主要工具，但采用 top-$k$ 样式激活函数的领先 SAE 方法缺乏选择超参数 $k$ 的理论基础。SAEs 基于线性表示假设（LRH），假设大型语言模型（LLMs）的表示是线性编码的，以及叠加假设（SH），说明模型中的特征数可以超过其维度。我们表明，基于 LRH 和 SH 的正式定义，稀疏特征向量（SAEs 从 LLM 的稠密嵌入中学习的潜在表示）的大小可以通过相应的稠密向量以闭式形式的误差界限进行估计。为了可视化这一点，我们提出了 ZF 图，该图揭示了 LLM 隐藏嵌入和 SAE 特征向量之间先前未知的关系，使我们能够首次对预训练 SAE 的特征向量在给定输入情况下的过度或不足激活程度进行实证测量。相应地，我们引入了近似特征激活（AFA），它估计真稀疏特征向量的大小，并提出了一种基于 AFA 的新评估指标来评估输入和激活之间的对齐。我们还利用 AFA 引入了一种新型 SAE 架构，top-AFA SAE，使得 SAEs：（a）在理论上更有依据；（b）不再需要调整 SAE 稀疏性超参数。最后，我们通过实证证明，top-AFA SAEs 实现了与最先进的 top-k SAEs 相当的重构损失，而无需调整超参数 $k$。我们的代码可在以下地址获取：https://github.com/SewoongLee/top-afa-sae。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是稀疏自编码器（SAEs）在现代机制可解释性中的重要性以及对于超参数 $k$ 的选择缺乏理论基础。

- (2): 过去的方法主要是应用如 top-k 这样的激活函数，但缺乏确保特征与输入嵌入之间对齐的有效方法，导致对输入的稀疏表示缺乏理论支持。提出的方法不同于现有方法，它引入了近似特征激活（AFA）并提出了 ZF 图，以可视化输入与特征激活之间的关系，从而解决了对齐问题。该方法在理论上有充分的动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于介绍了 AFA 方法，提供了一种以闭式形式估计稀疏特征激活大小的新理论，并提出了评估特征空间的 quasi-orthogonality 的新度量 εLBO，同时引入了 top-AFA 结构。

- (4): 本文提出的研究方法包括利用 AFA 进行特征激活的近似、使用 ZF 对特征激活进行可视化分析，以及设计一种无需调整超参数 $k$ 的顶层结构（top-AFA SAE）。

- (5): 该方法在重构损失上表现出色，达到了与最先进的 top-k SAE 相媲美的结果，支持了其实现稀疏自编码器有效性的目标。


## Learning Velocity and Acceleration: Self-Supervised Motion Consistency for Pedestrian Trajectory Prediction
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24272v1
- **Authors**: ['Yizhou Huang', 'Yihua Cheng', 'Kezhi Wang']
- **Abstrat**: Understanding human motion is crucial for accurate pedestrian trajectory prediction. Conventional methods typically rely on supervised learning, where ground-truth labels are directly optimized against predicted trajectories. This amplifies the limitations caused by long-tailed data distributions, making it difficult for the model to capture abnormal behaviors. In this work, we propose a self-supervised pedestrian trajectory prediction framework that explicitly models position, velocity, and acceleration. We leverage velocity and acceleration information to enhance position prediction through feature injection and a self-supervised motion consistency mechanism. Our model hierarchically injects velocity features into the position stream. Acceleration features are injected into the velocity stream. This enables the model to predict position, velocity, and acceleration jointly. From the predicted position, we compute corresponding pseudo velocity and acceleration, allowing the model to learn from data-generated pseudo labels and thus achieve self-supervised learning. We further design a motion consistency evaluation strategy grounded in physical principles; it selects the most reasonable predicted motion trend by comparing it with historical dynamics and uses this trend to guide and constrain trajectory generation. We conduct experiments on the ETH-UCY and Stanford Drone datasets, demonstrating that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance on both datasets.


**Translated Abstract**: 

理解人类运动对准确的行人轨迹预测至关重要。传统方法通常依赖监督学习，其中真实标签直接与预测轨迹进行优化。这放大了由长尾数据分布引起的局限性，使模型难以捕捉异常行为。在本文中，我们提出了一种自监督行人轨迹预测框架，该框架明确建模位置、速度和加速度。我们利用速度和加速度信息，通过特征注入和自监督运动一致性机制增强位置预测。我们的模型将速度特征层次注入到位置流中，加速度特征注入到速度流中。这使得模型能够联合预测位置、速度和加速度。从预测的位置中，我们计算相应的伪速度和加速度，使模型能够从数据生成的伪标签中学习，从而实现自监督学习。我们进一步设计了一种基于物理原则的运动一致性评估策略；通过将预测的运动趋势与历史动态进行比较，选择最合理的预测运动趋势，并使用该趋势指导和约束轨迹生成。在ETH-UCY和Stanford Drone数据集上的实验表明，我们的方法在这两个数据集上都达到了最先进的性能。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是行人轨迹预测，其在智能交通系统、自动驾驶、公共安全和人机交互等多个领域的重要性。

- (2): 过去的方法通常依赖于监督学习，通过计算损失与真实标签进行优化，这在长尾数据分布中存在问题，容易捕捉不到异常动态行为。所提方法通过自监督学习生成伪标签，从而避免了对真实标签的依赖，激发了更好的模型泛化能力。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出一种新颖的自监督运动一致性框架，能够从数据中自我学习结构模式，并在位置、速度和加速度的预测上实现协同建模。

- (4): 本文提出的研究方法是利用三流网络架构处理历史位置、速度和加速度数据，层次融合这些特征，并通过自监督机制强化运动一致性，提高预测的准确性。

- (5): 本文在ETH-UCY和Stanford Drone数据集上进行测试，达到了最先进的性能，验证了所提方法的有效性和目标的实现。


## Enhancing Image Resolution of Solar Magnetograms: A Latent Diffusion Model Approach
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24271v1
- **Authors**: ['Francesco Pio Ramunno', 'Paolo Massa', 'Vitaliy Kinakh', 'Brandon Panos', 'André Csillaghy', 'Slava Voloshynovskiy']
- **Abstrat**: The spatial properties of the solar magnetic field are crucial to decoding the physical processes in the solar interior and their interplanetary effects. However, observations from older instruments, such as the Michelson Doppler Imager (MDI), have limited spatial or temporal resolution, which hinders the ability to study small-scale solar features in detail. Super resolving these older datasets is essential for uniform analysis across different solar cycles, enabling better characterization of solar flares, active regions, and magnetic network dynamics. In this work, we introduce a novel diffusion model approach for Super-Resolution and we apply it to MDI magnetograms to match the higher-resolution capabilities of the Helioseismic and Magnetic Imager (HMI). By training a Latent Diffusion Model (LDM) with residuals on downscaled HMI data and fine-tuning it with paired MDI/HMI data, we can enhance the resolution of MDI observations from 2"/pixel to 0.5"/pixel. We evaluate the quality of the reconstructed images by means of classical metrics (e.g., PSNR, SSIM, FID and LPIPS) and we check if physical properties, such as the unsigned magnetic flux or the size of an active region, are preserved. We compare our model with different variations of LDM and Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic models (DDPMs), but also with two deterministic architectures already used in the past for performing the Super-Resolution task. Furthermore, we show with an analysis in the Fourier domain that the LDM with residuals can resolve features smaller than 2", and due to the probabilistic nature of the LDM, we can asses their reliability, in contrast with the deterministic models. Future studies aim to super-resolve the temporal scale of the solar MDI instrument so that we can also have a better overview of the dynamics of the old events.


**Translated Abstract**: 

太阳磁场的空间特性对于解码太阳内部及其对行星际影响的物理过程至关重要。然而，来自较旧仪器（如迈克尔逊多普勒成像仪，MDI）的观测具有有限的空间或时间分辨率，这妨碍了对小尺度太阳特征的详细研究。超分辨率处理这些旧数据集对于统一不同太阳周期的分析至关重要，这使得太阳耀斑、活跃区域和磁网络动态的特征更好地得到表征。在本研究中，我们提出了一种新型扩散模型的方法用于超分辨率，并将其应用于MDI磁图，以匹配中心波动成像仪（HMI）的更高分辨率。通过在下采样的HMI数据上训练带有残差的潜在扩散模型，并通过配对的MDI/HMI数据进行微调，我们能够将MDI观测的分辨率从2"/pixel提高到0.5"/pixel。我们通过经典度量（例如，PSNR、SSIM、FID和LPIPS）评估重建图像的质量，并检查未签名的磁通量或活跃区域的大小等物理特性是否得以保留。我们将这一模型与不同变体的LDM和去噪扩散概率模型（DDPMs）进行了比较，也与两种已经用于超分辨率任务的确定性架构进行了比较。此外，我们通过傅里叶域分析表明，带有残差的LDM能够解析小于2"的特征，由于LDM的概率特性，我们可以评估其可靠性，这与确定性模型形成对比。未来的研究旨在超分辨率处理太阳MDI仪器的时间尺度，以便更好地了解旧事件的动态。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究的背景是太阳磁场的空间特性，对于理解太阳内部物理过程及其对地球影响非常重要，但旧的观测仪器（如MDI）受限于空间和时间分辨率，影响了对小尺度太阳特征的研究。

- (2): 过去的方法主要是使用确定性模型进行超分辨率，存在无法有效处理低分辨率（LR）图像与高分辨率（HR）图像间不唯一映射的问题。本文提出的潜在扩散模型（LDM）通过引入残差机制来避免这些问题，使得模型能够生成更高质量的高分辨率图像，且可以提供输出的可信度评估。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出了一种新型的超分辨率方法，通过LDM显著改善了MDI磁图的图像分辨率，并在图像质量和物理特性保持方面达到了良好的效果。

- (4): 本研究的方法论包括在下采样的HMI数据上训练LDM并通过配对的MDI/HMI数据进行微调，使用经典指标（如PSNR、SSIM等）评估重建图像的质量，分析傅里叶域特征来确保输出图像的精确度。

- (5): 本文的方法在将MDI观测的分辨率从2"/pixel提升至0.5"/pixel的超分辨率任务上取得了显著性能。这一结果支持了作者的目标，即通过提高图像分辨率以促进对太阳动态的深入分析。


## New Statistical Framework for Extreme Error Probability in High-Stakes Domains for Reliable Machine Learning
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24262v1
- **Authors**: ['Umberto Michelucci', 'Francesca Venturini']
- **Abstrat**: Machine learning is vital in high-stakes domains, yet conventional validation methods rely on averaging metrics like mean squared error (MSE) or mean absolute error (MAE), which fail to quantify extreme errors. Worst-case prediction failures can have substantial consequences, but current frameworks lack statistical foundations for assessing their probability. In this work a new statistical framework, based on Extreme Value Theory (EVT), is presented that provides a rigorous approach to estimating worst-case failures. Applying EVT to synthetic and real-world datasets, this method is shown to enable robust estimation of catastrophic failure probabilities, overcoming the fundamental limitations of standard cross-validation. This work establishes EVT as a fundamental tool for assessing model reliability, ensuring safer AI deployment in new technologies where uncertainty quantification is central to decision-making or scientific analysis.


**Translated Abstract**: 

机器学习在高风险领域至关重要，但传统的验证方法依赖于平均指标，如均方误差（MSE）或平均绝对误差（MAE），无法量化极端错误。最坏情况下的预测失败可能产生重大后果，但当前的框架缺乏评估其概率的统计基础。本研究提出了一种基于极值理论（EVT）的新统计框架，提供了一种严谨的方法来估计最坏的失败。通过将EVT应用于合成和真实世界数据集，证明该方法能够稳健地估计灾难性失败的概率，克服了标准交叉验证的基本局限性。本研究确立了EVT作为评估模型可靠性的基本工具，从而确保了在不确定性量化对决策或科学分析至关重要的新技术中安全部署AI。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是机器学习在医疗诊断和自主系统等高风险应用中的重要性，强调理解和量化模型不确定性的重要性。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖MSE和MAE来验证模型性能，但这些方法无法捕捉极端错误。提出的方法通过引入EVT，解决了传统方法无法评估最坏情况预测失败的缺陷，具有良好的理论依据。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于建立了一种新的基于EVT的统计框架，用于极端错误概率的评估，从而提高机器学习模型在高风险环境中的可靠性和安全性。

- (4): 本文的方法论涉及将数据分为训练集和验证集，使用训练集训练模型，计算验证集上的误差，并应用EVT对极端误差进行建模和分析。

- (5): 本文的方法在合成和真实数据集上进行了应用，验证了该方法在估计极端错误概率方面的有效性，为高风险应用中的决策提供了有力支持。


## Advances in Continual Graph Learning for Anti-Money Laundering Systems: A Comprehensive Review
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24259v1
- **Authors**: ['Bruno Deprez', 'Wei Wei', 'Wouter Verbeke', 'Bart Baesens', 'Kevin Mets', 'Tim Verdonck']
- **Abstrat**: Financial institutions are required by regulation to report suspicious financial transactions related to money laundering. Therefore, they need to constantly monitor vast amounts of incoming and outgoing transactions. A particular challenge in detecting money laundering is that money launderers continuously adapt their tactics to evade detection. Hence, detection methods need constant fine-tuning. Traditional machine learning models suffer from catastrophic forgetting when fine-tuning the model on new data, thereby limiting their effectiveness in dynamic environments. Continual learning methods may address this issue and enhance current anti-money laundering (AML) practices, by allowing models to incorporate new information while retaining prior knowledge. Research on continual graph learning for AML, however, is still scarce. In this review, we critically evaluate state-of-the-art continual graph learning approaches for AML applications. We categorise methods into replay-based, regularization-based, and architecture-based strategies within the graph neural network (GNN) framework, and we provide in-depth experimental evaluations on both synthetic and real-world AML data sets that showcase the effect of the different hyperparameters. Our analysis demonstrates that continual learning improves model adaptability and robustness in the face of extreme class imbalances and evolving fraud patterns. Finally, we outline key challenges and propose directions for future research.


**Translated Abstract**: 

金融机构根据法规要求报告与洗钱相关的可疑金融交易。因此，他们需要不断监控大量进出交易。在洗钱检测中，一个特定的挑战是洗钱者不断调整他们的策略以逃避检测。因此，检测方法需要不断进行微调。传统机器学习模型在新数据上微调时容易遭受灾难性遗忘，从而限制了它们在动态环境中的有效性。持续学习方法可以解决这个问题并增强当前的反洗钱（AML）实践，因为它允许模型在保留先前知识的同时整合新信息。然而，关于 AML 的持续图学习研究仍然很稀缺。在这项综述中，我们批判性地评估了用于 AML 应用的最先进的持续图学习方法。我们将方法分为基于重放、基于正则化和基于架构的策略，并提供深入的实验评估，展示不同超参数的影响。我们的分析表明，持续学习提高了模型在极端类不平衡和不断演变的欺诈模式下的适应性和鲁棒性。最后，我们概述了主要挑战并提出了未来研究的方向。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是金融机构需要有效检测与洗钱相关的可疑交易，但洗钱者的手段不断变化，传统机器学习模型在新数据上微调时容易忘记旧的知识。

- (2): 过去的方法主要是基于传统机器学习模型，面临灾难性遗忘的问题。提出的方法是持续学习方法，能够在整合新信息的同时保留旧知识，从而解决了传统方法的不足。该方法对于动态的反洗钱（AML）系统具有良好的动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献包括对持续图学习在欺诈检测中的应用进行了深入的文献回顾，引入了持续图学习的关键概念，并提供了针对 AML 的实验结果。

- (4): 本研究的方法论包括文献综述和大量实验，分析超参数对模型表现和知识遗忘的影响。

- (5): 该方法在两个开源 AML 数据集上进行了评估，展示了在处理极端类不平衡和动态欺诈模式时的有效性，支持了其改进反洗钱系统的目标。


# AGN
## Unveiling the Fast Acceleration of AGN-Driven Winds at Kiloparsec Scales
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24359v1
- **Authors**: ['Cosimo Marconcini', 'Alessandro Marconi', 'Giovanni Cresci', 'Filippo Mannucci', 'Lorenzo Ulivi', 'Giacomo Venturi', 'Martina Scialpi', 'Giulia Tozzi', 'Francesco Belfiore', 'Elena Bertola', 'Stefano Carniani', 'Elisa Cataldi', 'Avinanda Chakraborty', "Quirino D'Amato", 'Enrico Di Teodoro', 'Anna Feltre', 'Michele Ginolfi', 'Bianca Moreschini', 'Nicole Orientale', 'Bartolomeo Trefoloni', 'Andrew King']
- **Abstrat**: Supermassive black holes at the centre of galaxies gain mass through accretion disks. Models predict that quasi-spherical winds, expelled by the black hole during active accretion phases, have a key role in shaping galaxy evolution by regulating star formation, the distribution of metals over kiloparsec scales, and by sweeping ambient gas to the outskirts and beyond of galaxies. Nonetheless, the mechanism driving these outflows and the amount of energy exchanged between the wind and the galaxy's interstellar medium remain unclear. Here, we present a detailed analysis of the kinematical properties of winds in a sample of nearby active galaxies using the novel kinematic tool MOKA3D, which takes into account the clumpy nature of the ISM. We find remarkable similarities among the properties of the outflows in all the galaxies examined. In particular, we provide the first evidence that outflows exhibit a regular trend in radial velocity, initially constant or slightly decreasing, followed by rapid acceleration starting at approximately 1 kpc from the nucleus, despite the seemingly complex kinematics observed. The observed behavior aligns with our current theoretical understanding of Active Galactic Nuclei outflows, where a momentum-driven phase transitions to an energy-conserving phase just beyond approximately 1 kpc. The constant velocity of the momentum-driven wind is then rapidly accelerated following the inefficient Compton cooling of post-shock material and the transition to energy conservation. The measured radial terminal velocities of the outflows are always larger than the escape velocities from the host galaxies, confirming the key role of outflows in shaping the galaxy properties and evolution, as a manifestation of AGN feedback. Our results, only made possible by our novel kinematic analysis tool, are crucial to understand the origin and the powering mechanism of these winds.


**Translated Abstract**: 

超大质量黑洞在星系中心通过吸积盘获得质量。模型预测，在黑洞活跃吸积阶段，排出的准球形风在塑造星系演化中发挥关键作用，这通过调节恒星形成、金属分布在千秒差距尺度上，以及清扫周围气体到星系的边缘及其外部。然而，驱动这些喷流的机制以及风与星系的星际介质之间的能量交换量仍不清楚。在这里，我们利用新颖的运动学工具MOKA3D，对一组附近活跃星系中的风的运动学特性进行详细分析。我们发现所检查的所有星系的喷流性质有显著相似之处。特别地，我们首次提供了证据，显示喷流在径向速度上表现出规律趋势，最初是恒定或稍有下降，然后在距离核约1千秒差距处迅速加速，尽管观察到的运动学似乎复杂。观察到的行为与当前对活跃星系核（AGN）喷流的理论理解一致，其中动量驱动阶段在约1千秒差距处转变为能量守恒阶段。动量驱动的风的恒定速度在后续的迅速加速中超越了逃逸速度，验证了喷流在塑造星系特性和演化中的关键作用，以及AGN反馈的表现。我们的结果只因我们新颖的运动学分析工具而得以可能，至关重要于理解这些风的起源和驱动机制。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究背景为超大质量黑洞的吸积及其在星系演化中的作用，特别是黑洞喷发的风如何调节恒星形成和气体分布。

- (2): 以前的方法主要依赖于简化的运动学模型，未能充分揭示喷流的复杂性和其与星际介质的相互作用。本文提出的方法MOKA3D考虑了星系中气体的块状特性，能够更准确地分析喷流运动学，从而解决了先前方法在复杂运动学描述上的不足，具有较强的理论动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于首次提供了AGN驱动喷流在千秒差距范围内加速的证据，揭示了动量驱动向能量守恒阶段的过渡，并确认了喷流在塑造星系特性中的关键角色。

- (4): 本文的研究方法为使用MOKA3D工具，分析附近活跃星系中喷流的运动学特性，利用光学积分场光谱仪MUSE进行数据采集和处理，以实现对喷流和星系盘的运动模型化。

- (5): 本文针对AGNs中喷流的运动学特性进行了分析，准确测量了喷流的径向终端速度，总体结果支持其在驱动星系演化过程中的重要作用。


## Gravitational Waves from Massive Black Hole Mergers in ASTRID: Predictions for LISA
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24304v1
- **Authors**: ['Bonny Y. Wang', 'Yihao Zhou', 'William Chen', 'Nianyi Chen', 'Tiziana Di Matteo', 'Rupert Croft', 'Simeon Bird', 'Yueying Ni']
- **Abstrat**: We use the ASTRID cosmological simulation to forecast massive black hole (MBH) binary mergers detectable by LISA. A key result is a significant increase in the predicted detection rate when MBH orbital eccentricity is included, rising from 5.6 for circular orbits to 10.5 events per year. This boost is largely due to inspiral sources that will merge after LISA's mission period, which make up 46% of detections in the eccentric case. This highlights LISA's sensitivity to early inspiral phases, especially for eccentric binaries that emit across a wider frequency band. Most LISA detections arise from $M_{\mathrm{BH}} \sim 10^{5-6}~\mathrm{M}_{\odot}$, low-redshift ($z<2$), low mass-ratio ($q\sim 0.01$--$0.1$) mergers, complementing instruments like Pulsar Timing Arrays (PTAs). Eccentricity also expands the detectable MBH mass range to $10^9~\mathrm{M}_{\odot}$ (from $10^8~\mathrm{M}_{\odot}$), and shifts the redshift peak from $z = 1.9$ (circular) to $z = 0.8$ (eccentric). We find LISA will detect MBH mergers in diverse host galaxies, including lower-mass and satellite galaxies. These hosts are $\sim 50$ times more star-forming than typical galaxies of the same mass, forming a tight power-law in SFR--$M_{\rm gal}$ space: ${\rm SFR} = 10^{-8} M_{\rm gal}^{0.9}~\mathrm{M}_{\odot}\,\mathrm{yr}^{-1}$, independent of redshift. This contrasts with expectations for PTA sources, which tend to reside in massive central galaxies, suggesting LISA will probe distinct galactic environments. Only $\sim 10\%$ of the remnant MBHs are bright AGNs, mostly from mergers with $M_{\mathrm{BH}} > 10^{6.5}~\mathrm{M}_{\odot}$.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们使用ASTRID宇宙学模拟来预测可被LISA探测到的巨型黑洞（MBH）双星合并。一个关键结果是，当考虑MBH轨道离心率时，预测的探测率显著增加，从圆形轨道的每年5.6次增加到10.5次。这一提升主要源于将要在LISA观测期之后合并的引导来源，在离心案例中占到了检测数量的46%。这突显了LISA对早期引导阶段的敏感性，尤其是对于在更宽频率范围内发射的离心双星。大多数LISA探测事件来自于质量约为10^5-6~M⊙、低红移（z<2）和低质量比（q~0.01--0.1）的合并，补充了脉冲星定时阵列（PTA）等仪器的观测。考虑轨道离心率还将可探测的MBH质量范围扩大到约10^9~M⊙（原本为10^8~M⊙），并将可探测合并的红移峰从圆形轨道的z=1.9降至离心轨道的z=0.8。我们发现，LISA将在多样的宿主星系中探测到MBH合并事件，包括低质量星系和卫星星系。这些宿主的星形成速率比相同质量的典型星系高出约50倍，在星形成速率-银河质量空间中形成紧密的幂律关系：SFR=10^{-8}M_{\rm gal}^{0.9}~M⊙/yr，与红移无关。这与PTA源的预期形成对比，后者往往位于大质量中心星系中，这表明LISA将探索发生在不同星系环境中的MBH合并事件。仅约10%的残余MBH是明亮的活动星核（AGN），大多数来自于质量大于10^{6.5}~M⊙的合并。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究了巨型黑洞（MBH）双星合并在宇宙学模拟ASTRID中的预测，旨在了解可由LISA探测到的MBH合并事件的特征和频率。

- (2): 过去的方法主要基于简化模型，忽视了MBH轨道的离心率，这限制了对合并事件的准确预测。本文的方法通过包含MBH的离心率，提升了探测率，并实现了对引导来源的更全面跟踪，从而解决了传统方法面临的预测精度问题。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于显著提高了预测的LISA探测事件率，并且详细探讨了离心率对可探测MBH合并事件的影响，揭示了不同星系环境下的MBH合并特征。

- (4): 本文采用ASTRID宇宙学模拟来动态建模MBH的轨道演化，考虑了MBH的离心率，并通过直接建模的方式，捕捉其在合并前的动态行为。

- (5): 研究表明，该方法预计每年可探测到10.5次MBH合并事件，较之前的5.6次有了显著提升。该性能足以支持对早期引导阶段的敏感探测目标，以及对不同星系环境中MBH合并的深入探索。


## Environmental effects in stellar mass gravitational wave sources I: Expected fraction of signals with significant dephasing in the dynamical and AGN channels
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24084v1
- **Authors**: ['Lorenz Zwick', 'János Takátsy', 'Pankaj Saini', 'Kai Hendriks', 'Johan Samsing', 'Christopher Tiede', 'Connar Rowan', 'Alessandro A. Trani']
- **Abstrat**: We present the first overview of the expected quantity of signals which will showcase significant gravitational wave phase shifts caused by astrophysical environments, considering the upcoming A+ and A\# LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA, Cosmic Explorer and Einstein Telescope detectors. We construct and analyse two general families of dephasing prescriptions with extensions to eccentric sources, as well as collect five specific prescriptions for the fundamental smoking gun physical mechanisms at play in the dynamical and AGN formation channel for stellar mass binary black holes: Roemer delays, tidal forces and hydrodynamical interactions. We compute the expected fraction of signals containing astrophysical dephasing, as a function of environmental properties and based on observed distributions of binary parameters. We find that next generation detectors can expect to find environmental effects in hundreds of detected signals.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们对即将到来的A+和A# LIGO/Virgo/KAGRA、Cosmic Explorer和Einstein Telescope探测器中，预期将展示由天体环境引起的显著引力波相位偏移的信号数量进行了首次全面概述。我们构建并分析了两组一般的相位偏移处方，并对五个关于在动态和AGN（活动星系核）形成通道中作用至关重要的物理机制的具体处方进行了收集：罗默延迟、潮汐力和流体动力学相互作用。我们根据观察到的双星参数分布，计算了包含天体相位偏移的信号的预期比例。我们发现下一代探测器可以预期在数百个检测信号中发现环境效应。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是重力波（GW）探测领域，尤其是围绕双黑洞（BBH）天体的形成途径和可观测特性的问题仍待解答。

- (2): 过去的方法主要集中于基于群体的统计推理，难以区分不同环境的特征与黑洞双星固有特性间的变化。本文提出的接近环境效应（EE）的方法，从少数GW信号中提取天体物理信息，能更好地识别相位偏移，克服了传统统计方法的局限性，且具有较强的动机。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于系统性地分析了动态与AGN通道中，导致引力波相位偏移的多种机制，并计算了在不同环境属性下包含天体相位偏移信号的预期比例。

- (4): 本文所提出的研究方法是通过有效估计天体源、环境和探测器属性下的引力波扰动的相关性，使用δSNR标准进行广泛的参数空间调查，识别可能出现EE的区域。

- (5): 本文的任务是评估不同环境条件下的引力波信号的可检测性，结果显示，在下一代探测器中数以百计的信号可能包含环境效应，支持了探讨信号中的天体信息的目标。


## Amoeba: An AGN Model of Optical Emissions Beyond steady-state Accretion discs
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2410.19630v2
- **Authors**: ['Henry Best', "Matthew O'Dowd", 'Joshua Fagin', 'James H. H. Chan', 'Bridget Ierace']
- **Abstrat**: Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN) are objects located in the heart of galaxies which emit powerful and complex radiation across the electromagnetic spectrum. Understanding AGN has become a topic of interest due to their importance in galactic evolution and their ability to act as a probe to the distant Universe. Within the next few years, wide-field surveys such as the Legacy Survey of Space and Time (LSST) at the Rubin Vera Observatory are expected to increase the number of known AGN to $\mathcal{O} (10^{7})$ and the number of strongly lensed AGN to $\mathcal{O} (10^{4})$. In this paper we introduce \texttt{Amoeba}: an AGN Model of Optical Emission Beyond steady-state Accretion discs. The goal of \texttt{Amoeba} is to provide a modular and flexible modelling environment for AGN, in which all components can interact with each other. Through this work we describe the framework for major AGN components to vary self-consistently and keep flux distributions to connect these components to spatial dependent processes. We model properties beyond traditional single-component models, such as the reverberation of the corona's bending power law power spectrum through the accretion disc and broad line region (BLR). We simulate obscuration by the dusty torus and differential magnification of the disc and BLR due to microlensing. These features are joined together to create some of the most realistic light curve simulations to date. \texttt{Amoeba} takes a step forward in AGN modelling by joining the accretion disc, BLR, torus, intrinsic signal, and microlensing into a coherent model.


**Translated Abstract**: 

活跃星系核（AGN）是位于星系中心的天体，在电磁波谱上发出强大而复杂的辐射。理解AGN已成为一个重要的研究话题，因为它们在星系演化中的重要性以及它们能够作为探测遥远宇宙的工具。预计在接下来的几年中，鲁宾维拉天文台的广域巡天（Legacy Survey of Space and Time, LSST）将使已知的AGN数量增加到$\mathcal{O} (10^{7})$，以及强透镜AGN的数量增加到$\mathcal{O} (10^{4})$。本文介绍了\texttt{Amoeba}：一种超出稳态吸积盘的光学发射AGN模型。 \texttt{Amoeba}的目标是提供一个模块化和灵活的AGN建模环境，各个组件可以相互作用。通过这一工作，我们描述了主要AGN组件自洽变化的框架，并保持通量分布以将这些组件连接到空间依赖的过程。我们模拟了尘埃托勒的遮蔽以及由于微透镜作用而导致的光盘和宽线区（BLR）的差异放大。这些特征结合在一起创造出迄今为止最为真实的光曲线模拟。\texttt{Amoeba}在AGN建模中迈出了新的一步，将吸积盘、BLR、托勒、内在信号和微透镜结合成一个连贯的模型。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究的背景是活跃星系核（AGN）的强大辐射及其在星系演化和遥远宇宙探测中的重要性。

- (2): 以往的模型通常基于单一组件，无法捕捉AGN复杂的相互作用。这些方法存在的主要问题是缺乏灵活性和自洽性。而本文提出的\texttt{Amoeba}模型能够模块化地处理多个组件间的相互作用，极大地提高了模型的真实性。

- (3): 纸中的贡献在于提出了一种新的AGN建模框架，将多个物理成分（吸积盘、BLR、尘埃托勒和微透镜）整合在一起，提供了更为准确的光曲线模拟。

- (4): 本文提议的研究方法是开发一个模块化的模拟环境，允许各个AGN组件的自洽变化，并考虑空间依赖过程的通量分布。

- (5): 该论文的结果在生成真实的AGN光曲线模拟方面表现优异，支持其在可信度与准确度上设定的目标。


## Modelling variability power spectra of active galaxies from irregular time series
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2501.05886v2
- **Authors**: ['Mehdy Lefkir', 'Simon Vaughan', 'Daniela Huppenkothen', 'Phil Uttley', 'Vysakh Anilkumar']
- **Abstrat**: A common feature of Active Galactic Nuclei (AGN) is their random variations in brightness across the whole emission spectrum, from radio to $\gamma$-rays. Studying the nature and origin of these fluctuations is critical to characterising the underlying variability process of the accretion flow that powers AGN. Random timing fluctuations are often studied with the power spectrum; this quantifies how the amplitude of variations is distributed over temporal frequencies. Red noise variability -- when the power spectrum increases smoothly towards low frequencies -- is ubiquitous in AGN. The commonly used Fourier analysis methods, have significant challenges when applied to arbitrarily sampled light curves of red noise variability. Several time-domain methods exist to infer the power spectral shape in the case of irregular sampling but they suffer from biases which can be difficult to mitigate, or are computationally expensive. In this paper, we demonstrate a method infer the shape of broad-band power spectra for irregular time series, using a Gaussian process regression method scalable to large datasets. The power spectrum is modelled as a power-law model with one or two bends with flexible slopes. The method is fully Bayesian and we demonstrate its utility using simulated light curves. Finally, Ark 564, a well-known variable Seyfert 1 galaxy, is used as a test case and we find consistent results with the literature using independent X-ray data from XMM-Newton and Swift. We provide publicly available, documented and tested implementations in Python and Julia.


**Translated Abstract**:  
活跃星系核（AGN）的一个共同特征是它们在整个发射光谱中随机的亮度变化，从无线电波到γ射线。研究这些波动的性质和起源对表征驱动AGN的吸积流的底层变化过程至关重要。随机时序波动通常通过功率谱进行研究，该谱量化了变化幅度在时间频率上的分布。在AGN中，红噪声变异性——即功率谱向低频平滑增加——是普遍存在的。常用的傅里叶分析方法在处理不规则采样的红噪声光曲线时面临重大挑战。虽然存在几种时域方法可以推断功率谱形状，但它们存在难以缓解的偏差或计算上代价高昂的问题。本文展示了一种使用高斯过程回归方法推断不规则时间序列的宽带功率谱形状的新方法，该方法可扩展至大数据集。功率谱建模为具有一个或两个弯曲的幂律模型，并具有灵活的斜率。该方法是完全贝叶斯的，我们通过模拟光曲线证明其效用。最后，使用著名的可变 Seyfert 1 星系 Ark 564 作为测试案例，我们发现与文献中通过独立的 XMM-Newton 和 Swift 数据得到的一致结果。我们提供了可公开获取、文档齐全且经过测试的 Python 和 Julia 实现。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究活跃星系核（AGN）的亮度变化及其与吸积流的关系，以获得对黑洞物理特性的理解。

- (2): 过去的方法主要是傅里叶分析，适用于规则采样，但在处理不规则采样的红噪声时面临挑战。虽然有时域方法可用，但它们存在偏差和高计算成本的问题。本文提出的高斯过程回归方法能够处理大规模数据集，弥补了传统方法的不足，提供了一种更有效的功率谱推断方式。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于提出了一种新的贝叶斯推断方法，以处理不规则采样数据的宽带功率谱，并通过对标志性AGN Ark 564实证验证了该方法。

- (4): 本文使用高斯过程回归方法建立功率谱模型，以幂律形式描述有一个或两个弯曲的形状。

- (5): 本文在分析不规则时间序列的宽带功率谱方面取得了成功，验证结果与现有文献一致，证明了其方法的有效性和可靠性。


## X-ray cavities in TNG-Cluster: a direct comparison to observations
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.01965v2
- **Authors**: ['Marine Prunier', 'Annalisa Pillepich', 'Julie Hlavacek-Larrondo', 'Dylan Nelson']
- **Abstrat**: The TNG-Cluster magnetohydrodynamic cosmological simulations, produce a diverse population of X-ray cavities in the intracluster medium (ICM) of simulated galaxy clusters. These arise from episodic, high velocity, kinetic energy injections from the central active supermassive black hole (AGN, SMBH). Here, we present the first comprehensive comparative analysis of X-ray cavities in TNG-Cluster with observational data. First, we select a volume-limited sample of 35 real clusters ($z \leq 0.071$, M$_\text{500c}$ = 10$^{14-14.8}$ M$_\odot$) observed with the Chandra X-ray Observatory, identify 3 analogs for each in TNG-Cluster (total of 105) and generate mock Chandra images using same exposure times as their observed counterparts. We identify X-ray cavities and measure their properties in both datasets using identical techniques, ensuring a direct, apples-to-apples comparison. Our analysis reveals that both samples have a similar fraction of X-ray cavities (35-43 per cent). They exhibit comparable sizes and morphologies, although the sizes of simulated X-ray cavities still attached to the SMBH are somewhat larger in TNG-Cluster -- a scarcity at $< 10$ kpc. The area of TNG X-ray cavities increases as they rise in the ICM, consistent with the trend seen in the observational sample. The cavity powers, estimated using observational techniques, show good agreement between the two samples (10$^{42-45}$ erg.s$^{-1}$), suggesting that X-ray cavities in the simulation are an important heating mechanism in cluster cores. Overall, the rather simple AGN feedback model of TNG, with no model choices made to reproduce X-ray morphological features, and without cosmic rays, creates a quantitatively realistic population of X-ray cavities at cluster scales.


**Translated Abstract**: 

TNG-Cluster磁流体动力学宇宙模拟产生了一种多样的X射线空腔群体，这些空腔位于模拟的星系团的星系间介质（ICM）中。它们源于来自中央活跃超大质量黑洞（AGN，SMBH）的间歇性高速度动能注入。我们在这里展示了TNG-Cluster中X射线空腔与观测数据的首次全面比较分析。首先，我们选择了一个有限体积的样本，包含35个真实星系团（𝑧 ≤ 0.071，M500c = 10^14−14.8 M⊙），并为每个星系团在TNG-Cluster中识别出3个类比（总共105个），生成与其观测相对比的模拟Chandra图像。我们使用相同的技术，在两个数据集中识别X射线空腔并测量它们的性质，从而确保进行了直接、一对一的比较。我们的分析表明，这两个样本具有相似的X射线空腔比例（35-43%）。它们在大小和形态上也表现出可比性，尽管TNG-Cluster中仍然附着在SMBH上的模拟X射线空腔的大小略大——在10 kpc以下较少。有意思的是，TNG X射线空腔的面积随着它们在ICM中上升而增加，这与观测样本的趋势一致。使用观测技术估计的空腔功率表明两者间的良好一致性（10^42−45 erg.s^−1），这表明模拟中的X射线空腔是星系团核中重要的加热机制。总体而言，TNG的相对简单的AGN反馈模型，并未为重现X射线形态特征而做出模型选择，也没有涉及宇宙射线，创造出在星系团尺度上数量上相对现实的X射线空腔群体。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究的背景是星系团中的复杂物理过程，以及活跃超大质量黑洞（AGN）对星系团核心的影响，特别是在星系间介质（ICM）中形成的X射线空腔。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖于观测数据，通过Chandra X射线天文台分析X射线空腔。然而，这些方法未能直接比较模拟和观测之间的X射线空腔特征。本文提出的方法通过比较TNG-Cluster模拟与实际观测数据，确保使用相同的技术对空腔进行一对一分析，从而解决了以前方法的局限性，具有强烈的理论基础。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于首次全面比较TNG-Cluster模拟的X射线空腔与实际观测数据，结果表明模拟中的X射线空腔在物理性质上与观测样本相符，进一步验证了AGN反馈作为加热机制的重要性。

- (4): 本文的研究方法包括选择35个真实星系团样本，并为每个样本在TNG-Cluster中找到3个对应的模拟对象，生成相同曝光时间的模拟Chandra图像，使用相同技术进行X射线空腔的识别和性质测量。

- (5): 本文的方法在比较X射线空腔的比例、尺寸和功率上取得了良好性能（功率范围10^42−45 erg.s^−1），这些结果支持了其目标，即深入理解AGN反馈对星系团演化的影响。


## Narrow-Line Seyfert 1 Galaxies Beyond the Local X-ray Universe: An X-ray spectral sample
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.23849v1
- **Authors**: ['Jiachen Jiang', 'Dominic J. Walton', 'Luigi C. Gallo', 'Andrew C. Fabian', 'Dirk Grupe', 'Richard McMahon', 'Christopher S. Reynolds', 'Andrew Young', 'Zhibo Yu', 'Honghui Liu', 'Zuobin Zhang']
- **Abstrat**: Narrow-line Seyfert 1 AGNs (NLS1s) represent a unique stage in the black hole growth history, characterised by low black hole masses of approximately $10^{6}$-$10^{8}$ solar masses and around-Eddington accretion rates. X-ray studies of NLS1s have largely been confined to the local Universe ($z < 0.2$), while their broad-line counterparts and radio-loud quasars have been more extensively investigated at higher redshifts. In this work, we conducted an X-ray spectral analysis for 14 SDSS-observed NLS1s at $z\approx1$ in the eRASS1 catalogue. We found that all of their eROSITA observations agree with the expected rest-frame 2 keV monochromatic luminosity given their rest-frame 2500 angstrom monochromatic luminosity, further supporting evidence of AGN emission. Second, when fitted with a power-law model, most continuum spectra between 0.7-7 keV in their rest frames necessitate photon indices $\Gamma\gtrsim2.5$. Notably, the highest photon index of around 4.7 in one of our NLS1 AGNs hints at a significant contribution from soft excess emission. Finally, our analysis demonstrates that we can align the Eddington ratios with optical measurements by applying a correction factor between 10-120 to their X-ray luminosity. Although measurement uncertainty remains considerable, our findings suggest that assumptions for the standard geometrically thin accretion disc model made in previous estimations of this correction factor may not apply to near or super-Eddington NLS1 AGNs. Finally, we also compare this sample with extremely variable nearby NLS1s and other X-ray-weak AGNs, such as JWST-observed, broad-line AGNs at $z=5-6$, and underscores the importance of deeper X-ray surveys for more X-ray-weak NLS1s.


**Translated Abstract**: 

窄线塞非尔1类活动星系核（NLS1s）代表了黑洞增长历史中一个独特的阶段，特点是黑洞质量约为 $10^{6}$-$10^{8}$ 倍太阳质量和接近爱丁顿极限的吸积率。对NLS1s的X射线研究在很大程度上限于局部宇宙（$z < 0.2$），而其宽线对应物和强射电 Quasar 在更高红移下得到了更广泛的研究。在这项工作中，我们对$z \approx 1$的14个SDSS观测的NLS1s进行了X射线光谱分析，这是以eRASS1目录为基础。我们发现它们的所有eROSITA观测都与其静止参考帧2500埃单色光度所预期的静止参考帧2 keV单色光度一致，进一步支持了活动星系核辐射的证据。其次，当用功率律模型拟合时，大多数在其静止参考框架内的光谱连续发送（0.7-7 keV）需要光子指数$\Gamma \gtrsim 2.5$。特别地，我们的一个NLS1 AGN的最高光子指数约为4.7，暗示了软 excess 辐射的显著贡献。最后，我们的分析表明，通过在其X射线光度上应用一个10-120的修正因子，我们可以将爱丁顿比率与光学测量对齐。尽管测量不确定性仍然相当大，我们的结果表明，在之前估算这一修正因子时所做的标准几何薄吸积盘模型的假设可能不适用于接近或超爱丁顿的NLS1 AGNs。最后，我们还将这一样本与极为变动的附近NLS1s和其他X射线弱的AGN进行比较，比如在$z=5-6$的JWST观测的宽线AGN，并强调了对更多X射线弱NLS1s进行更深X射线调查的重要性。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是窄线塞非尔1类活动星系核（NLS1s）在黑洞增长历史中的独特性，其特点是具有较低的黑洞质量（$10^{6}$-$10^{8}$倍太阳质量）和接近爱丁顿的吸积率。

- (2): 过去的研究方法主要集中在局部宇宙中的NLS1s（$z<0.2$），难以研究较高红移的对象。该文提出的新方法针对$z\approx1$的NLS1s进行系统的X射线光谱分析，克服了以往研究中红移限制的问题。所提方法合理性强，针对性的修正因子使得光学测量与X射线光度对齐。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于首次针对$z\approx1$的14个NLS1s进行了详尽的X射线光谱分析，支持了活动星系核的辐射模型，并发现高光子指数提示软excess的存在。

- (4): 本文的研究方法是通过对eROSITA和SDSS数据的结合，使用功率律模型对NLS1s的X射线光谱进行拟合，从而深入分析其光度、光子指数等参数。

- (5): 在所分析的14个NLS1s中，发现大部分的光谱连续发送需要光子指数$\Gamma \gtrsim 2.5$，这表明在近或超爱丁顿的NLS1 AGNs中，标准吸积盘模型的假设并不适用，支持了本文的研究目标。


## Predicting Sunyaev-Zel'dovich effect observations of galaxy cluster cavities with the Square Kilometre Array
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.23599v1
- **Authors**: ['Sophia Geris', 'Yvette Perrott']
- **Abstrat**: Galaxy cluster X-ray cavities are inflated by relativistic jets that are ejected into the intracluster medium by active galactic nuclei (AGN). AGN jets prevent predicted cooling flow establishment at the cluster centre, and while this process is not well understood in existing studies, simulations have shown that the heating mechanism will depend on the type of gas that fills the cavities. Thermal and non-thermal distributions of electrons will produce different cavity Sunyaev Zel'dovich (SZ) effect signals, quantified by the 'suppression factor' f. This paper explores potential enhancements to prior constraints on the cavity gas type by simulating suppression factor observations with the Square Kilometre Array (SKA). Cluster cavities across different redshifts are observed to predict the optimum way of measuring f in future observations. We find that the SKA can constrain the suppression factor in the cavities of cluster MS 0735.6+7421 (MS0735) in as little as 4 h, with a smallest observable value of f~0.42. Additionally, while the SKA may distinguish between possible thermal or non-thermal suppression factor values within the cavities of MS0735 if it observes for more than 8 h, determining the gas type of other clusters will likely require observations at multiple frequencies. The effect of cavity line of sight (LOS) position is also studied, and degeneracies between LOS position and the measured value of f are found. Finally, we find that for small cavities (radius < 80 kpc) at high redshift (z~1.5), the proposed high frequencies of the SKA (23.75-37.5 GHz) will be optimal, and that including MeerKAT antennas will improve all observations of this type.


**Translated Abstract**: 

星系团X射线空腔是由活跃星系核（AGN）喷射的相对论性喷流向星系团介质中膨胀形成的。AGN喷流阻止了在星系团中心形成预测的冷却流，尽管这一过程在现有研究中尚不清楚，但模拟表明加热机制将取决于填充空腔的气体类型。热和非热的电子分布将产生不同的空腔Sunyaev-Zel'dovich (SZ)效应信号，通过“抑制因子”f量化。本文通过模拟使用平方千米阵（SKA）观察抑制因子，探讨了对现有空腔气体类型约束的潜在增强。观察不同红移的星系团空腔，预测未来观察f的最佳测量方式。我们发现，SKA可以在短至4小时内限制星系团MS 0735.6+7421 (MS0735)的空腔抑制因子，最小可观测值约为f ~ 0.42。此外，如果SKA观察超过8小时，可能区分MS0735空腔内的热或非热抑制因子值，而确定其他星系团的气体类型可能需要在多个频率下进行观察。还研究了空腔视线位置的影响，并发现视线位置与测得f值之间的简并性。最后，我们发现对于高红移(z ~ 1.5)的小空腔（半径<80 kpc），SKA的高频范围（23.75-37.5 GHz）将是最佳的，并且包括MeerKAT天线将提升所有此类观察的效果。

**Summary**:


- (1): 本文研究星系团X射线空腔的性质，这些空腔是由AGN喷流在星系团介质中形成的，影响了星系团的加热机制和冷却流的发展。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖于观测和模拟来约束空腔内气体类型，但对气体成分的理解仍不够深入，存在限制。本文提出的使用SKA观测抑制因子的方法可以更优化地测量空腔气体性质，从而解决了过往方法的不足。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于通过模拟展示了SKA如何有效地约束MS0735星系团空腔的抑制因子，提高了对AGN喷流气体成分的理解。

- (4): 本文采用了计算机模拟的方法，通过SKA对星系团不同红移空腔进行观察，预测最佳的抑制因子测量方案。

- (5): 本文的方法在预测MS0735的抑制因子方面，最小值约为f ~ 0.42，并能够在4小时内获得有效测量，这充分支持了研究目标。


# ALMA
## ALMA Band 3 Selection of Ultra-high Redshift Dropouts: The final challenge to ΛCDM
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24312v1
- **Authors**: ['C. Lovell', 'M. Lee', 'A. Vijayan', 'T. Harvey', 'L. Sommovigo', 'A. Long', 'E. Lambrides', 'W. Roper', 'S. Wilkins', 'D. Narayanan', 'N. Adams', 'D. Austin', 'M. Maltz']
- **Abstrat**: The Lyman-break technique has been used to successfully identify high-redshift candidates in broad-band photometric data in the rest-frame optical and NIR using the dropout technique. We pioneer the application of this technique to new wavelength regimes, and search for dropouts in combined ALMA and JWST data. We find a candidate that is undetected in NIRCam imaging including and blueward of the F444W filter, but clearly identified in ALMA band 3. Assuming this is a Lyman-break candidate, we measure a redshift in the range $40 < z < 21\,380$. This is the highest redshift galaxy candidate discovered to date, and is in significant tension with current and future predictions from cosmological simulations, with implications for galaxy evolution in the (very) early Universe.


**Translated Abstract**: 

Lyman-break 技术已成功用于在宽光谱光度数据中识别高红移候选者，涉及到射电和近红外波段的断点技术。我们开创性地将此技术应用于新的波长范围，并在联合 ALMA 和 JWST 数据中搜索断点。我们发现一个候选者在 NIRCam 成像中未被检测到，包括 F444W 过滤器及其蓝侧，但在 ALMA B3 中清晰可见。在假设这是一个 Lyman-break 候选者的基础上，我们测量了红移范围 $40 < z < 21,380$。这是迄今为止发现的最高红移星系候选者，且与当前和未来的宇宙模拟预测存在显著的矛盾，影响早期宇宙中的星系演化。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是 Lyman-break 技术用于高红移星系候选者的识别，特别是在不断逼近高红移的研究中。

- (2): 过去的方法依托于 NIR 数据进行 Lyman-break 选择，但在 z > 15 的候选者中存在许多误判。提出的方法结合了 ALMA 和 JWST 数据，从而利用更广泛的波长范围搜索候选者，减轻了对低红移星系的误识别风险，提供更可靠的红移估计。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于发现了一个红移范围高达 $40 < z < 21,380$ 的候选星系，这是当前已知的最高红移星系候选者，并且该发现对现有的宇宙学模型提出了挑战。

- (4): 本文中的研究方法包括利用 ALMA B3 数据与 JWST 的近红外数据整合，针对特定波长范围的断点进行精细的光谱分析，实现高红移星系的识别和红移测量。

- (5): 该方法在识别超高红移星系候选者的任务中取得了显著表现，发现突破性红移候选者这一结果能够支持他们在早期宇宙形成过程的研究上的目标。


## The edge-on disk Tau042021: icy grains at high altitudes and a wind containing astronomical PAHs
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.24309v1
- **Authors**: ['E. Dartois', 'J. A. Noble', 'M. K. McClure', 'J. A. Sturm', 'T. L. Beck', 'N. Arulanantham', 'M. N. Drozdovskaya', 'C. C. Espaillat', 'D. Harsono', 'M. -E. Palumbo', 'Y. J. Pendleton', 'K. M. Pontoppidan']
- **Abstrat**: Spectra of the nearly edge-on protoplanetary disks observed with the JWST have shown ice absorption bands of varying optical depths and peculiar profiles, challenging radiative transfer modelling and our understanding of dust and ice in disks. We build models including dust grain size, shape, and composition to reproduce JWST IFU spectroscopy of the large edge-on disk Tau042021. We explore radiative transfer models using different dust grain size distributions, including grains of effective radii a_eff = 0.005-3000 microns. Scattering properties of distributions of triaxial ellipsoidal grains are calculated. We consider compositions with silicates, amorphous carbon, and mixtures of H2O, CO2, and CO. We use RADMC-3D Monte Carlo radiative transfer models of Tau042021 to simulate the spectral cubes observed with JWST-NIRSpec and MIRI. We compare the results to observations, including H2O at 3.05 microns, CO at 4.67 microns, and CO2 at 4.27 microns and to archival JWST-NIRCam and ALMA continuum images. The observed near- to mid-infrared imply dust distributions with grain sizes up to several tens of microns. The intensity distribution perpendicular to the disk exhibits emission profile wings extending into the upper disk atmosphere at altitudes exceeding the classical scale height expected in the isothermal hydrostatic limit. We produce ice map images demonstrating the presence of icy dust grains up to altitudes high above the disk midplane, more than three hydrostatic equilibrium scale heights. We demonstrate the presence of a wind containing the carriers of astronomical PAH bands. The wind appears as an X-shaped emission at 3.3, 6.2, 7.7 and 11.3 microns, characteristic wavelengths of the infrared astronomical PAH bands. We associate the spatial distribution of this component with carriers of astronomical PAH bands that form a layer of emission at the interface with the H2 wind.


**Translated Abstract**: 

通过使用JWST观察的几乎边缘视角的原行星盘的光谱，发现冰的吸收带具有不同的光学深度和奇特的轮廓，这使得辐射传输模型和我们对盘中尘埃和冰的理解面临挑战。我们构建了包括尘埃颗粒的大小、形状和组成的模型，以重现JWST IFU对大边缘盘Tau042021的光谱观测。我们探索使用不同的尘埃颗粒尺寸分布的辐射传输模型，考虑了有效半径在0.005到3000微米之间的颗粒。我们计算了triaxial椭球颗粒分布的散射特性，考虑了包含硅酸盐、无定形碳以及水、二氧化碳和一氧化碳的混合物的组成。利用RADMC-3D蒙特卡洛辐射传输模型模拟Tau042021的光谱立方体，并将结果与观测数据进行比较，包括3.05微米的H2O，4.67微米的CO和4.27微米的CO2。观察到的近红外到中红外光谱表明尘埃分布包含尺寸达到几十分米的颗粒。垂直于盘的强度分布显示出发射轮廓的延伸，超出经典等温气体静力平衡的尺度高度。我们生成冰映射图像，证明冰尘颗粒存在于高于盘中平面的高度，超过三个静力平衡尺度高度。我们展示了包含天文学PAH带载体的风的存在，该风在3.3、6.2、7.7和11.3微米处表现为X形辐射。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究背景是利用JWST观测几乎边缘视角的原行星盘，以探讨冰和尘埃的分布以及辐射传输模型的复杂性。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖简单的辐射传输模型，难以解释观察到的光谱特征和尘埃分布。本文提出的方法通过构建更复杂的模型，包含尘埃颗粒的多种特性，以克服这些问题，显示出对复杂光谱特征的更好拟合。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于揭示了Tau042021盘中冰尘颗粒应能够高于中平面存在，且存在承载天文学PAH带的盘风，这有助于深入理解原行星盘中物质的分布与动态。

- (4): 本文的研究方法是建立包含尘埃颗粒大小、形状和组成的辐射传输模型，利用RADMC-3D蒙特卡洛方法模拟JWST的光谱立方体，并进行观测数据的对比。

- (5): 本文的方法在解析冰和尘埃的空间分布及其光谱特征方面表现出显著的成功，支持了研究的目标，即揭示复杂盘中尘埃和气体的物理结构。


## A grand-design spiral galaxy with an ordered magnetic field at redshift 2.6 as resolved with ALMA and gravitational lensing
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2412.08705v3
- **Authors**: ['W. de Roo', 'S. Vegetti', 'D. M. Powell', 'S. W. Ndiritu', 'R. Pakmor', 'J. P. McKean']
- **Abstrat**: Magnetic fields play an important role in the evolution of galaxies and in shaping the dynamics of their inter-stellar medium. However, the formation history of magnetic fields from initial seed-fields to well-ordered systems is not clear. Favoured scenarios include a turbulent dynamo that amplifies the field, and a mean-field dynamo that organizes it. Such a model can be tested through observing the magnetic-field structure of galaxies in the early Universe given the relative formation time-scales involved. Here, we combine the high angular resolution of the Atacama Large Milli-metre Array (ALMA) and gravitational lensing to resolve the magnetic field structure of a 4-kpc in extent grand-design spiral when the Universe was just 2.6 Gyr old. We find that the spiral arm structure, as traced by the heated dust emission, is coincident with the linearly polarized emission, which is consistent with a highly ordered magnetic field. The time-scale needed to produce such an ordered field is likely within at least several rotations of the disk. Our study highlights the importance of combining the long baselines of ALMA and gravitational lensing to resolve the structure of galaxies at cosmologically interesting epochs.


**Translated Abstract**: 

磁场在星系的演化中扮演着重要的角色，并塑造其星际介质的动态。然而，从初始种子场到有序系统的磁场形成历史尚不清楚。常见的场景包括一种湍流发电机增强磁场，以及一种均值场发电机组织磁场。这样的模型可以通过观察早期宇宙中星系的磁场结构来测试。本文结合了阿塔卡马大毫米波阵列（ALMA）的高角分辨率和引力透镜效应，以解析一个在宇宙仅有26亿年历史时的、延展4千秒差距的典型螺旋星系的磁场结构。我们发现，螺旋臂结构与线性偏振辐射相吻合，这与高度有序的磁场一致。产生如此有序场所需的时间尺度可能在磁盘的至少几次旋转范围内。我们的研究突显了结合ALMA的长基线和引力透镜以解析宇宙中有趣时代的星系结构的重要性。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文研究的背景是磁场在星系演化和星际介质动态中的重要性，尤其是其空间结构的理解。

- (2): 过去的方法主要依赖于极化热辐射的间接测量，但在高红移星系中，由于辐射微弱和分辨率较低，面临挑战。本文提出的结合ALMA和引力透镜的新方法解决了这些问题，并允许对早期宇宙中的磁场结构进行高分辨率观察。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于解析了一个典型螺旋星系在高红移下的磁场结构，发现了与高度有序磁场一致的结果。

- (4): 研究方法包括使用ALMA的高分辨率观测以及通过引力透镜增强信号，以解析目标星系的磁场结构。

- (5): 本文任务是在红移2.6下研究星系的磁场结构，所获得的结果支持了其目标，即理解星系早期磁场的形成和演化。

Gutierrez', 'A. Hall', 'S. Hemmati', 'H. Hildebrandt', 'J. Hjorth', 'A. Jimenez Muñoz', 'J. J. E. Kajava', 'V. Kansal', 'D. Karagiannis', 'C. C. Kirkpatrick', 'A. M. C. Le Brun', 'J. Le Graet', 'J. Lesgourgues', 'T. I. Liaudat', 'A. Loureiro', 'J. Macias-Perez', 'G. Maggio', 'M. Magliocchetti', 'F. Mannucci', 'R. Maoli', 'J. Martín-Fleitas', 'C. J. A. P. Martins', 'L. Maurin', 'R. B. Metcalf', 'M. Miluzio', 'P. Monaco', 'A. Montoro', 'A. Mora', 'C. Moretti', 'G. Morgante', 'Nicholas A. Walton', 'L. Patrizii', 'V. Popa', 'D. Potter', 'I. Risso', 'P. -F. Rocci', 'M. Sahlén', 'E. Sarpa', 'C. Scarlata', 'A. Schneider', 'M. Sereno', 'F. Shankar', 'P. Simon', 'A. Spurio Mancini', 'J. Stadel', 'S. A. Stanford', 'K. Tanidis', 'C. Tao', 'G. Testera', 'R. Teyssier', 'S. Toft', 'S. Tosi', 'A. Troja', 'M. Tucci', 'C. Valieri', 'J. Valiviita', 'D. Vergani', 'G. Verza', 'P. Vielzeuf']
- **Abstrat**: The Euclid mission is generating a vast amount of imaging data in four broadband filters at high angular resolution. This will allow the detailed study of mass, metallicity, and stellar populations across galaxies, which will constrain their formation and evolutionary pathways. Transforming the Euclid imaging for large samples of galaxies into maps of physical parameters in an efficient and reliable manner is an outstanding challenge. We investigate the power and reliability of machine learning techniques to extract the distribution of physical parameters within well-resolved galaxies. We focus on estimating stellar mass surface density, mass-averaged stellar metallicity and age. We generate noise-free, synthetic high-resolution imaging data in the Euclid photometric bands for a set of 1154 galaxies from the TNG50 cosmological simulation. The images are generated with the SKIRT radiative transfer code, taking into account the complex 3D distribution of stellar populations and interstellar dust attenuation. We use a machine learning framework to map the idealised mock observational data to the physical parameters on a pixel-by-pixel basis. We find that stellar mass surface density can be accurately recovered with a $\leq 0.130 {\rm \,dex}$ scatter. Conversely, stellar metallicity and age estimates are, as expected, less robust, but still contain significant information which originates from underlying correlations at a sub-kpc scale between stellar mass surface density and stellar population properties.


**Translated Abstract**: 

Euclid 任务生成了大量高角分辨率的四个广泛滤光器的成像数据。这将允许对星系的质量、金属丰度和恒星种群进行详细研究，从而限制它们的形成和演化路径。将 Euclid 成像转换为大样本星系的物理参数图是一个重要的挑战。我们研究了机器学习技术在提取良好分辨率星系内部物理参数分布方面的能力和可靠性。我们专注于估计恒星质量表面密度、质量加权恒星金属丰度和年龄。我们为 1154 个来自 TNG50 宇宙模拟的星系生成了在 Euclid 光谱带下的无噪声合成高分辨率成像数据。图像是使用 SKIRT 辐射传输代码生成的，考虑了恒星种群的复杂 3D 分布和星际尘埃衰减。我们使用机器学习框架将理想化的模拟观测数据逐像素映射到物理参数。我们发现，恒星质量表面密度可以准确恢复，散射小于 0.130 {\rm \,dex}。相反，恒星金属丰度和年龄估计的稳健性较差，但仍含有重要信息，这些信息源自恒星质量表面密度与恒星种群特性之间在亚千秒差距尺度上的内在关联。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是宇宙学领域对星系演化的理解，特别是通过 Euclid 任务获取的高分辨率成像数据对星系质量、金属丰度和恒星种群的研究。

- (2): 过去的方法主要是通过拟合模板谱能分布（SED）来估计星系的物理属性，但这种方法通常无法充分考虑星系内部的复杂结构，导致在分辨率上存在不足。本文提出了一种机器学习的方法，该方法通过逐像素的方式、在模拟的高质量数据基础上进行物理参数的准确提取，能够解决以上问题，并充分考虑星系的非均匀性。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于首次使用机器学习技术对从 Euclid 任务生成的星系成像数据提取恒星质量表面密度、金属丰度和星龄，提供了一个高效且可靠的框架。

- (4): 研究方法针对 1154 个星系的模拟数据，生成无噪声图像，并使用机器学习框架逐像素映射至物理参数，重点在于通过复杂的 3D 恒星分布和星际尘埃衰减进行分析。

- (5): 本文的方法在恒星质量表面密度的恢复上达到了小于 0.130 {\rm \,dex} 的散射，虽然对星际金属丰度和年龄估计的稳健性不如前者，但仍包含重要信息，表明本文方法有助于实现对星系物理参数的精确提取。


## Kiloparsec-Scale Alignment of a Radio Jet with Cool Gas and Dust in a z~6 Quasar
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.23797v1
- **Authors**: ['Fabian Walter', 'Eduardo Banados', 'Chris Carilli', 'Marcel Neeleman', 'Thomas Connor', 'Roberto Decarli', 'Emanuele Paulo Farina', 'Yana Khusanova', 'Chiara Mazzucchelli', 'Romain Meyer', 'Emmanuel Momjian', 'Hans-Walter Rix', 'Sofia Rojas-Ruiz', 'Bram Venemans']
- **Abstrat**: We present high-angular resolution (0.068", ~400pc) ALMA imaging of the [CII] line and dust continuum emission of PSO J352.4034-15.3373, a radio-loud quasar at z=5.83. The observations reveal a remarkably close match between the orientation of the [CII] and thermal dust emission mapped by ALMA, and radio synchrotron emission of a radio jet previously mapped by the VLBA. This narrow alignment extends over ~4kpc, reminiscent of the well-studied 'alignment effect' in lower-redshift radio galaxies. The [CII] kinematics show a linear increase in velocity with galactocentric radii up to ~200 km/s at r=2kpc, consistent with bulk motions within the galaxy potential, and not relativistic jet motions. The kinematics and respective morphologies are consistent with a picture in which the relativistic jet injects energy into the interstellar medium (potentially leading to subsequent star formation), giving rise to the observed alignment and significant (> 100 km/s) [CII] velocity dispersion within the host galaxy on kiloparsec scales. Indeed, the astonishingly close alignment and narrow linearity of the radio jet with the [CII] and dust emission are hard to conceive without some fundamental relationship between the two.


**Translated Abstract**: 

我们呈现了对 z = 5.83 的射电明亮类星体 PSO J352.4034–15.3373 进行的高角度分辨率（0.068″，约400 pc）ALMA 探测的 [C II] 线和尘埃连续发射的成像。这些观测揭示了 ALMA 映射的 [C II] 和热尘埃发射方向与通过 VLBA 先前映射的射电喷流的同步辐射发射之间的显著匹配。这种狭窄对准延伸至约 4 kpc，令人想起低红移射电星系中广泛研究的“对准效应”。[C II] 的运动学显示速度随星系中心距离线性增加，在 r = 2 kpc 时达到约 200 km/s，符合星系势能内的整体运动，而不是相对论喷流运动。运动学及相关形态与一种图景一致，即相对论喷流向星际介质注入能量（可能导致后续的恒星形成），产生观察到的对准及主星系内显著的 (> 100 km/s) [C II] 速度色散。确实，射电喷流与 [C II] 和尘埃发射之间的惊人对准和狭线性难以想象，而二者之间必定存在某种基本关系。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是对 z ≳ 6 类星体（如 PSO J352.4034–15.3373）的观测，这些类星体挑战了我们对早期超大质量黑洞和星系形成的理解。 

- (2): 过去的方法是使用低分辨率观测对类星体的星际介质进行探测，结果在寻找中央超大质量黑洞与星系主机之间的相互作用方面存在局限。本文通过高分辨率 ALMA 成像，建立了 [C II]、尘埃与射电喷流之间的紧密对准，解决了过去方法所面临的问题并展示了二者之间的关系。

- (3): 论文的贡献在于首次呈现了一个高红移类星体中，射电喷流与星际介质（[C II] 和尘埃）之间的明确对准，表明相对论喷流可能影响星系内的气体运动并促进星形成。

- (4): 本文的研究方法是通过高角度分辨率的 ALMA 探测对 PSO J352.4034–15.3373 的 [C II] 线和尘埃发射进行成像，得到了关于运动学和形态的信息。

- (5): 该方法在识别和分析 [C II] 及尘埃数据时取得了显著的表现，显示出射电喷流与星系内气体之间的关系，从而支持了其研究目标。


## Dual-band Unified Exploration of Three CMZ Clouds (DUET). Cloud-wide census of continuum sources showing low spectral indices
- **Url**: http://arxiv.org/abs/2503.23700v1
- **Authors**: ['Fengwei Xu', 'Xing Lu', 'Ke Wang', 'Hauyu Baobab Liu', 'Adam Ginsburg', 'Tie Liu', 'Qizhou Zhang', 'Nazar Budaiev', 'Xindi Tang', 'Peter Schilke', 'Suinan Zhang', 'Sihan Jiao', 'Wenyu Jiao', 'Siqi Zheng', 'Beth Jones', 'J. M. Diederik Kruijssen', 'Cara Battersby', 'Daniel L. Walker', 'Elisabeth A. C. Mills', 'Jens Kauffmann', 'Steven N. Longmore', 'Thushara G. S. Pillai']
- **Abstrat**: The Milky Way's Central Molecular Zone (CMZ) is measured to form stars 10 times less efficiently than in the Galactic disk, based on emission from high-mass stars. However, the CMZ's low-mass protostellar population, which accounts for most of the initial stellar mass budget and star formation rate (SFR), is poorly constrained observationally due to limited sensitivity and resolution. We present the Dual-band Unified Exploration of Three CMZ Clouds (DUET) survey, targeting the 20 km/s Cloud, Sgr C, and Dust Ridge cloud e using the Atacama Large Millimeter/submillimeter Array (ALMA) at 1.3 and 3 mm. The mosaicked observations achieve a comparable resolution of 0.2-0.3" (~1600-2500 au) and a sky coverage of 8.3-10.4 square arcmin, respectively. We report 563 continuum sources at 1.3 mm and 330 at 3 mm, respectively, and a dual-band catalog with 450 continuum sources. These sources are marginally resolved at the 2,000 au resolution. We find a cloud-wide deviation (>70%) from commonly-used dust modified blackbody (MBB) models, characterized by either low spectral indices or low brightness temperatures. Three possible explanations for the deviation are discussed. (1) Optically thick Class 0/I Young stellar objects (YSOs) with very small beam filling factors can lead to lower brightness temperatures than what MBB models predict. (2) Large (mm/cm-sized) dust grains have more significant self-scattering, and therefore frequency-dependent albedo could cause lower spectral indices. (3) Free-free emission over 30 uJy can severely contaminate dust emission and cause low spectral indices for mJy sources in our sample, although the needed number of massive protostars (embedded UCHII regions) is infeasibly high for the normal stellar initial mass function. A reliable measurement of the SFR at low protostellar masses will require future work to distinguish between these possible explanations.


**Translated Abstract**: 

银河系的中心分子区（CMZ）根据高质量恒星的发射，形成恒星的效率被测定为仅为银河盘的十分之一。然而，由于敏感性和分辨率的限制，CMZ的低质量原恒星群体（大约<2 M⊙）的观测约束较差，这一群体占据了初始恒星质量预算和恒星形成率（SFR）的主要部分。我们展示了三大CMZ云的双波段统一探索（DUET）调查，目标为20 km/s云、Sgr C和Dust Ridge云，使用阿塔卡马大型毫米/亚毫米阵列（ALMA）在1.3和3 mm波段进行观测。这些马赛克观测达到0.2-0.3"（约1600-2500 au）的分辨率和8.3-10.4平方弧分的天空覆盖率。我们报告在1.3 mm处发现563个连续源，在3 mm处发现330个，并提供一个包含450个连续源的双波段目录。这些源在2000 au分辨率下是边缘分辨的。我们发现，超过70%的样本在已普遍使用的尘埃改良黑体（MBB）模型中存在普遍的偏差，表现为低谱指数或低亮度温度。我们讨论了三种可能的偏差解释。需要未来工作来区分这些可能的解释，以可靠地测量低原恒星质量的SFR。

**Summary**:

- (1): 本文的研究背景是银河系中心分子区（CMZ）尽管有大量的分子气体，但其恒星形成效率却极低，特别是对于低质量（<2 M⊙）的原恒星群体的观测约束存在不足。

- (2): 以往的方法依赖于自由-自由发射的测量，分辨率低且无法详细描绘低质量原恒星群体。本文提出的方法使用阿塔卡马大型毫米/亚毫米阵列（ALMA）进行高分辨率、多波段观测，大大提高了对低质量原恒星的检测能力，有效解决了传统方法中的灵敏度和分辨率问题。

- (3): 本文的贡献在于进行了一次云范围的原恒星普查，发现了563个和330个在不同波段的连续源，提出了对尘埃改良黑体模型偏差的可能解释，并为后续工作的SFR测量奠定了基础。

- (4): 本文采用的研究方法是使用ALMA进行1.3 mm和3 mm波段的马赛克观测，覆盖多个CMZ云，以高分辨率检测云内的连续源并分析其特点。

- (5): 本文研究探讨了CMZ云中的原恒星群体，达成高达563个和330个的源发现，虽然新发现的数据不完全符合预测的尘埃模型，但它为进一步研究CMZ的恒星形成率提供了可靠的基础，进而支持作者的目标。
